Weicheng Company Goes to Europe to Promote Silk

▲Appoints Legal Representative Bai Lisi as Chief Representative in Europe

Weicheng Company is a well-known silk merchant in China, whose products are known for their exquisite quality and are sold throughout East Asia, enjoying a high reputation. The company exports approximately 8,000 bales of silk to Europe and America annually, ranking third among Shanghai's raw silk export firms. To expand its business, it is also engaged in the export of domestic silk fabrics and various sundries. It has appointed its legal representative, Bai Lisi, as its chief representative in Europe to negotiate promotion matters in order to achieve direct exports and avoid being controlled by foreign merchants.

Appeal for Disaster Relief in Shan County, Shaanxi

▲Red Cross Receives Telegram from Shan County Party Consolidation Committee

The Chinese Red Cross Society received a telegram from the Party Consolidation Committee of Shan County, Henan Province, stating: "Our Henan Province is afflicted by natural and man-made disasters that come together, with no escape from bandits, locusts, droughts, and wars. Shanling County is the most severely affected. Since the great bandit Lao Yangren broke the city in the eleventh year, killing, burning, looting, and committing all kinds of atrocities, continuous warfare has followed, with no peaceful years. The people are exhausted and their suffering is indescribable. Last year, the rebel Feng Mutiny, occupying western Henan with hundreds of thousands of troops, relied entirely on our small and weak populace for support, supply, conscription, borrowing money, requisitioning grain, demolishing houses, and seizing livestock. Such acts of plunder by the troops were commonplace. The people endured a year of deep suffering. Our Shan County is on the verge of collapse. Heaven does not pity us and has added to our calamities with famine. Summer crops and autumn harvests have failed for consecutive years. The wealthy have no means to make a living, and the poor are wandering the roads. Now, in the cold winter, the post-disaster victims, how can they endure it? We hereby telegraphically appeal to all sectors for the people and hope that benevolent people will show compassion and generously donate grain and funds. Then, the hundreds of thousands of disaster victims in Shan County will be eternally grateful. The urgency of the telegram cannot express the eager anticipation.

Three Lost Children Awaiting Collection

▲Girl Wang Maomao: Zhang Guanghan, a guard policeman from the 17th post of the 1st District, 1st Sub-bureau of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, found a crying girl on the Bund at around 8:00 PM the night before and immediately brought her back to the sub-bureau. When questioned by the director of the sub-bureau, the girl stated that her name was Wang Maomao, three years old, from Haimen. Her father has returned to his hometown, and her mother is in Shanghai. She came out of her house today and lost her way home after playing in the street, so she was crying. She is being kept at the sub-bureau awaiting collection by her family.

▲Boy with No Name: Zhou Yintang, a guard policeman from the 1st post of the same sub-bureau, found a boy around 4 or 5 years old wandering on Xiaoputuo Bridge Street at around 5:00 PM yesterday afternoon. He was wearing a blue floral cloth jacket and pants, black socks, and blue cloth shoes, and had a flat-top haircut. He appeared to be lost and was immediately brought back to the sub-bureau. When questioned by the director of the sub-bureau, the boy refused to speak, so his family's name and address could not be determined. He is being kept at the sub-bureau awaiting collection.

▲Boy Qian Ayu: The Municipal Public Security Bureau reported yesterday that the 3rd sub-bureau of the 5th District had sent a lost boy named Qian Ayu. According to his statement, he is nine years old, from Shanghai, and cannot remember his home address. He has parents; his father's name is Qian Yinchang. This time, he went to visit relatives with his mother and got separated and lost on the way home. The boy was wearing a red felt hat, a floral foreign thread cloth jacket, a black cloth monk-collared vest, red cloth trousers, and black shoes. He was sent to the Xinpu Yutang (New General Welfare Hall) for foster care and a notice was posted to find his family.

Dafeng Daily to Be Published Tomorrow

The Dafeng Daily, a tri-daily newspaper organized by Xu Muyun and Xiao Ting, two brothers in the Shanghai literary and art circles, is scheduled to be published today. The writers, such as She Yu, Guo Yi, Ban Kuang, Huo Gong, Zi Bao, and Shao Qing, are all well-known figures. The illustrations by Ding Muqin and Wu Tianweng are particularly profound and incisive. The first issue contains two photographs taken during the transfer of Sun Yat-sen's remains to the Western Hills, featuring important figures from all sides. The content is extremely valuable. The issue coincides with the anniversary of Sun Yat-sen's death and is very timely. The second issue contains a portrait of Wu Mingyi, the fiancé of Zhang Biyue, the protagonist in the shooting of Huang Changxing. Zhang divorced Wu because of Huang's dissuasion and later learned that she had been deceived by Huang. Therefore, she shot Huang in anger. This matter caused a national sensation. The Shangyue Society even adapted it into a new play. Wu's demeanor must be something that the general public is eager to see. Zhang Biyue previously committed suicide at Datong University. Wu has written a long article for the newspaper, which will be revealed in the second issue. It is thought that the general reader will want to read it first.

Gentai Heye Flour Sells Well

The Gentai Heye Flour Factory, solely funded by the Shanghai magnate Cheng Linsheng, has a long history. Its Heye flour is rich in nutrients, exquisitely delicious, made of pure ingredients, and beneficial to health. Therefore, since its launch, it has sold well at home and abroad, and is praised as the king of condiments. Those who previously used imported products are now using domestic Heye flour across the board. Mr. Li Quanshen, the manager of the factory, is even more hardworking and serves as the technician, striving for delicious taste and white color for the products. Due to the strong sales, the factory is working day and night to step up production.

Lihua Company Did Not Establish a Savings Department

The Lihua Company received an official letter from the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday stating that the company also operates a savings department. The Lihua Company stated that it has been in business for six years, and the working capital used in previous years relied solely on the turnover of shares. It never engaged in savings activities. In the autumn of the 19th year, due to seeing shareholders and employees frequently adding small amounts of money, savings were attached to the coupon sales office. As of now, the total amount is less than 10,000 yuan, all added by shareholders and employees, which is absolutely not in the nature of savings. For the sake of prudence, the company has never advertised in newspapers or distributed printed materials to solicit savings. Moreover, since the Social Affairs Bureau issued an order to ban companies from also operating savings, the company was concerned that the savings would also be in conflict, so it had already stopped accepting deposits and was successively notifying shareholders and employees to withdraw their savings to avoid misunderstandings. The company plans to submit a document to the Social Affairs Bureau in the near future to report the above situation.

The Caishi Road plaque was inscribed with the words "Benefiting the Common People," and the Baxianqiao plaque was inscribed with the words "Guardian of the Citizens." At 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, all the vendors gathered at the Lianhehui (Joint Association) of the vegetable market in Xinle Lane, Nanyang Bridge. Representatives from Caishi Road, including Zhu Rui, Xu Guifang, and Huang Rendang, and representatives from Baxianqiao, including Dai Maotai, Wei Azhang, Yu Ade, and Chen Yunqing, led a procession with a military band in the front, followed by two pavilions. They went directly to the Shandong Guild Hall, which is the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association. The military music was melodious along the way, and firecrackers were set off. Upon arriving at the association, committee member Tong, secretary Shao, and clerk Shen came out to greet them and served tea and refreshments to the representatives. After some time, the representatives said goodbye and departed.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday: The sky is cloudy and overcast. There will be fog in the Yangtze River basin in the morning. Winds along the coast of the country are directionless. There is a cyclone between the Ryukyu Islands and the Ogasawara Islands. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 55.8 degrees, and the lowest was 31.1 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 56.7 degrees, and the lowest was 37.9 degrees.
